---

excalidraw-plugin: parsed
tags: [excalidraw]

==⚠  Switch to EXCALIDRAW VIEW in the MORE OPTIONS menu of this document. ⚠==


# Text Elements
Conflict:
Characters Ci and Cj are in Conflict if there exist four rows in the matrix such that these columns
contain all 4 combos (0,0), (0,1), (1,0), (1,1)
M is conflict free if no pairs of columsn i and j are in conflict

 ^aeJwwMLS

Theorem: A binary character state matrix M is conflict free if and only iff there exist a perfect phylognoT




Compatibility
Define S(ci) = set of specifes exhibiting character c

Characters ci and cj are pairwise compatible iff S(ci_ and S(cj_ are either disjoin
or one contains the other M is mutually compatible if all pair wise columns i
and j are pairwise compatible

Compatibility Graph G = (v,E)
V = set of characters
E = pairs of mutually compatible characters
Largest subset of compatible characters is the largest clique in G (Also NP-hard_


 ^BS3eKRE0

%%
